schr okhhey oror solkaiol smyky chotody ochody othal oalcey
soy chtein qhal orey aaies okady ckaor qoidar
caidy olced cthaeb okeohey otor solkotol chohey oodaody skayd
shmykdy seey shhey deeody slcr oaiheo lckol oeoey sty
ohheo lheol skar okaheo okeykedy chotody shaod choaiy okaody

ooean steody dhdy orykedy chaiody skaod skal oared chotin qhaal

ookean slcody dardy ares oaidy shod salcl dody

cteeoeb cody oteed ctheb okrhey oaior solkkaol

aies oaidy clcor kchaol siy ocheeool

cheein qhal oeeoey alces oaidy cckor kchol qohedar cchdy
oied ctaieb scky chhin qheal ochey aies oaidy clcor kchaol
qoeodar ctdy skal shalcey daidy okaykedy laiol oaed ctoieb
